I'm a 98 year old retiree who used to listen to bangers like this back in my day, in fact earlier this afternoon I was having lunch and thinking back on those times... see back then you didn't have as many options for lunch but you could count on it, they'd be piping hot and delicious, even back then sometimes I'd just go without eating... see without having any kind of manual labor to do, a fella like me never got that beach body that the young ladies were after, we'd have to go down to the docks and do push ups and use some of the equipment down there.. It was dangerous, let me tell you what, I remember one afternoon, it was blazing hot, somehow I just remember it being muggier back then.  We didn't have air conditioning in the houses like we do now, we'd just have to sweat it out, the ladies all had a personalized fan, that was all the rage for awhile... there were a few years where Oriental fashion was very big in some of the circles... I never had time for that of course, what with the arithmetic and what not, a fella got awful busy in the evenings.  I didn't have the natural ease at schooling like my older brother Robin did, oh he was so smug!  Dad always compared us and usually it felt awful until Robin's senior prom.  I was just a junior see, but I had been practicing some moves with some of the pep squad gals... when it came time for Robin to make his big debut, after sneaking a silver dollar and a recently acquired record to the DJ... the pep ladies and I stole the show with a revolutionary dance routine, set to a contemporary number called "Baddadan".  Boyyyy, you should have seen my spiteful brother's face when I led the whole crowd, tippin' and leaning, teaching them our new dance, which we called the "Douglas"... after Douglas McNarly, who unfortunately was at home with the Mumps that evening.

I still CANT BELIEVE how my car still intact. Yesterday this song came on and I almost crashed. I was speeding trying to go on green light but the red one came and the cars infront of me stoped. I was going to hit the car infront of me and in the last moment I changed to the right lane forcing the car there to change to the other right line. Then the car from there came upfront me and stopped. From there  one big and fat man with a baseball bat came on heading to me. The song was still banging and I told him: "Look bro, it is my fault for this incident, BADADAN came on and I though that I am invincible, sorry". He nodded his head and said: "I understand, be careful next time!" then we shook hands and he got back in his car. I was still shaking and thank god I am alive. Thank you Chase & Status for this amazing song,  next time, I'll really be careful!
